  <a href="/user/show/4821369-jolo-manansala" class="left imgcol" title="Jolo Manansala"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1342837849p2/4821369.jpg" alt="Jolo Manansala" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/311615894?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Apr 13, 2012</a>

      <a href="/user/show/4821369-jolo-manansala" class="user" title="Jolo Manansala">Jolo Manansala</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/115130.A_Stranger_In_The_Mirror" title="Paperback 9780006471257" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/4821369-jolo-manansala?shelf=favorites" class="actionLinkLite">favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer311615894">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8832090084438363029">This was my first ever Sidney Sheldon book and I loved it. I literally could not put the book down. I slept at 11 pm for three nights and finished it then. The suspense really got me every night and the only thing that kept me from reading was that I knew that I needed to wake up early in the morning. <br /><br />Never has a book made me feel so much emotions in one time. I felt the passion, the hate, the love, and to be honest, I felt turned on (Blame it on my fourteen year old hormones) at the well-explai</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8832090084438363029">This was my first ever Sidney Sheldon book and I loved it. I literally could not put the book down. I slept at 11 pm for three nights and finished it then. The suspense really got me every night and the only thing that kept me from reading was that I knew that I needed to wake up early in the morning. <br /><br />Never has a book made me feel so much emotions in one time. I felt the passion, the hate, the love, and to be honest, I felt turned on (Blame it on my fourteen year old hormones) at the well-explained sex scenes.<br /><br />Every word made me want to read the next. Even the prologue made me want to read the whole book that instant. I wanted to find out what would happen to Toby, what would happen to Jill. I saw their transgression from nobodies, one with a huge organ and one I really thought was going to die with her headaches. I loved every minute of it. I loved every minute of reading the book.<br /><br />The last few scenes gave me chills. It was probably due to the fact I was reading at 11 pm. The words were just written so well. I can't even describe how I felt. <br /><br />It really was great and I can't wait to buy another Sidney Sheldon book. The fact that he's a Tony winner made me like him more.<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8799456341762081929">** spoiler alert ** I could give Sidney Sheldon's books 5 stars without even reading them because I know they're all gonna be great! <br />"A Stranger in the Mirror" is another amazing story by this amazing author. I got really annoyed when I had to put it down. The story is absolutely breathtaking!<br />It's about a boy "Toby" and a girl "Jill" who wanted to leave their hometowns to find fame in Hollywood. Terrible things happen to them along the way. The girl seeks revenge when she finally becomes an impo</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8799456341762081929">** spoiler alert ** I could give Sidney Sheldon's books 5 stars without even reading them because I know they're all gonna be great! <br />"A Stranger in the Mirror" is another amazing story by this amazing author. I got really annoyed when I had to put it down. The story is absolutely breathtaking!<br />It's about a boy "Toby" and a girl "Jill" who wanted to leave their hometowns to find fame in Hollywood. Terrible things happen to them along the way. The girl seeks revenge when she finally becomes an important person. The boy forgets about his past and enjoys his success and turns into a jerk.<br />It's like two stories in one book. The amazing part is, when these two "Toby and Jill" get together in the last few chapters... Don't want to spoil the ending for you guys. So, buy it, read it, and thank me later ;)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15294404946016855824">Mr. Sheldon does it again! Another breathtaking story about love, betrayal, vengeance and murder. This is bit different than his other books but I really enjoyed it.<br /><br />Toby grew up with an idea that he was born to be famous. On the other hand, Jill grew up dreaming about being rich and beautiful. Soon, both realize that the only place that gives them what they want is Hollywood.<br /><br />Both of them have to struggle to reach to the top. The part that describes their struggle is really heart touching. They h</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText15294404946016855824">Mr. Sheldon does it again! Another breathtaking story about love, betrayal, vengeance and murder. This is bit different than his other books but I really enjoyed it.<br /><br />Toby grew up with an idea that he was born to be famous. On the other hand, Jill grew up dreaming about being rich and beautiful. Soon, both realize that the only place that gives them what they want is Hollywood.<br /><br />Both of them have to struggle to reach to the top. The part that describes their struggle is really heart touching. They have to lie, face humiliation, get rejected and sell their bodies until they get chance. Soon Toby becomes the superstar and the king of Hollywood but Jill is still struggling until one day they cross each other's path. Despite their age difference, they fall in love. Toby wants to marry Jill because she was the only girl who ever rejected him but Jill wants him because getting Toby's power is the only way to punish all the people who have used and rejected her.<br /><br />They rise and rise as a Golden Couple of Hollywood until the love turns into betrayal and betrayal influences vengeance. The hounding carries on until they come together again, and until their love story is written forever by the stars that are only visible to soft night wind and the timeless sea.<br /><br />Sidney Sheldon gets 5 out of 5 again from me.<br /><br />Published on <a rel="nofollow" href="http://pchhantyal.blogspot.in/2014/10/a-stranger-in-mirror-by-sidney-sheldon.html" target="_blank">http://pchhantyal.blogspot.in/2014/10...</a></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer426888753">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1786361271357423730">Ah, Sidney Sheldon, what can you say about him? His novels are trashy, full of unrealistic, rather silly plots, sex and situations ... and they are so un-putdownable that they might as well be made of crazy glue. <br /><br />In this one, two young aspiring performers have simultaneous stories. Toby Temple is a young comic with a boyish, innocent face but a mean streak a mile deep. Jill Castle has had to fight and claw to get any sort of career. <br /><br />This one gets three stars rather than just one because the stor</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText1786361271357423730">Ah, Sidney Sheldon, what can you say about him? His novels are trashy, full of unrealistic, rather silly plots, sex and situations ... and they are so un-putdownable that they might as well be made of crazy glue. <br /><br />In this one, two young aspiring performers have simultaneous stories. Toby Temple is a young comic with a boyish, innocent face but a mean streak a mile deep. Jill Castle has had to fight and claw to get any sort of career. <br /><br />This one gets three stars rather than just one because the story genuinely surprised me and it was immensely readable and enjoyable to me. There was stuff, especially in the last third, that I simply did not see coming and I loved how Sheldon pulled it all together. It gets three stars instead of five because of the clunky pacing in the first half and the ridiculously schmaltzy romantic language. <br /><br />It's like cotton candy - I'll have forgotten the characters' names by next week (actually, I had to look up Jill's last name just to write this review). But I love cotton candy. </span>

  <span style="display:none" id="freeText17155910879145124317">Well..its my 5th Sidney Sheldon book. I could not rate less than 5 stars in any of his books so far. Here, Toby Temple captures the title "the most funniest man in the world" though he passed through many loathsome folks in his path. On the other hand, Jill Castle who also had an ambition but partial talent, uses Toby to reach her heights. Selfish love, revenge, hatred, betraying were brought out in a marvelous way. The tale was really interesting that i was reading contiguously skipping my appetite. The rapid situations and suspense did not allow me to guess the climax at all. To emphasize on the whole book it was a tremendous book with overwhelming characters. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11872524471335411302">I am in the process of re-reading my Sidney Sheldon book collection. I haven't read these books for many years and thought it would fun to go back try them again. <br /><br />I'd actually give this book somewhere between 2-3 stars. This book has just about everything...starting with poor humble beginnings to pride,greed,revenge,sex - a lot of sex,consequences of choices made....and much more. I don't think this is one of Sheldon's better plots. It was interesting but didn't hold my interest for very long. I</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText11872524471335411302">I am in the process of re-reading my Sidney Sheldon book collection. I haven't read these books for many years and thought it would fun to go back try them again. <br /><br />I'd actually give this book somewhere between 2-3 stars. This book has just about everything...starting with poor humble beginnings to pride,greed,revenge,sex - a lot of sex,consequences of choices made....and much more. I don't think this is one of Sheldon's better plots. It was interesting but didn't hold my interest for very long. It was very easy for me to put down the book or quickly become distracted by other things, which is unsually for me when I am reading.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13711586553345458812">This is so different from Sheldon's books. And while we know this story will end in a tragic way, I had to complete it!<br />It is compelling, intriguing, well-informed, and in the end, justified - for we sure don't want to have a negative feeling like "They got away..."<br /><br />And Sheldon has taken care of that. We kn</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText13711586553345458812">This is so different from Sheldon's books. And while we know this story will end in a tragic way, I had to complete it!<br />It is compelling, intriguing, well-informed, and in the end, justified - for we sure don't want to have a negative feeling like "They got away..."<br /><br />And Sheldon has taken care of that. I kept hoping things might get better, but I knew they wouldn't, for it's always a good thing that we remember where we came from, how great we grow...<br />And the characters are strongly drawn out. We know them like we saw them... And this story haunted me...than any book I ever read.<br />And though I felt depressed by the story line, I thought about it a lot and knew that this one is a great book, because, it doesn't give false hopes, and it is one that made me kept reading though the characters weren't really the nicest persons in the world.<br /><br />A deep story that says truth isn't a sweet fruit always... Reality bites... We just have to be careful in the beginning itself....<br />I give it four stars...<br /></span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_409679009">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/409679009" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/3929792-vaultofbooks" class="left imgcol" title="VaultOfBooks"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1348989948p2/3929792.jpg" alt="VaultOfBooks" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/409679009?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Sep 07, 2012</a>

      <a href="/user/show/3929792-vaultofbooks" class="user" title="VaultOfBooks">VaultOfBooks</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="did not like it">did not like it</span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="did not like it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/115130.A_Stranger_In_The_Mirror" title="Paperback 9780006471257" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer409679009">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2299704324132038733">By Sidney Sheldon. Grade: C<br />Sidney Sheldon is time and time again pitted as one of the world’s all-time best fiction novelist. From being an author to a screen writer to a producer, Sidney Sheldon has done it all and then some more. A Stranger in the Mirror, a fiction suspense novel, is the third of his career.<br />Toby Temple is a superstar, the world’s funniest man. He gets any woman that he wants, but under the superstar image is a lonely man. Jill Castle is a sensuous starlet. She has a dark and m</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText2299704324132038733">By Sidney Sheldon. Grade: C<br />Sidney Sheldon is time and time again pitted as one of the world’s all-time best fiction novelist. From being an author to a screen writer to a producer, Sidney Sheldon has done it all and then some more. A Stranger in the Mirror, a fiction suspense novel, is the third of his career.<br />Toby Temple is a superstar, the world’s funniest man. He gets any woman that he wants, but under the superstar image is a lonely man. Jill Castle is a sensuous starlet. She has a dark and mysterious past and has an ambition even greater than Toby’s. Together they rule Hollywood.<br /><br />The plot is not as simple as the synopsis. The plot follows the life and times of Toby Temple, a youngster born in the family of a German butcher who apparently is of no good and his mother has held the mantle of the house for a very long time. All through his teenage, he tries to make his mother happy. But (atypical of Sidney Sheldon style), his teenage was full of exploits, so to speak. A very innocent looking boy, he could have any girl and woman he wanted. But he had some other things in his sight.<br />He had harboured a childhood hobby of mimicking others and decided of making it big as an entertainer. In the beginning, he found it very hard to make ends meet. But then (with some serious help of his charm and looks) he finds two people who change his life. He finally makes it big.<br />On the other hand, Jill Castle a.k.a. Josephine Czinski, born to a poor family (she gave a hard time being born) never wanted to do anything extraordinary. But a personal tragedy pushed her into the streets of Hollywood which then became her ultimate fantasy. But she couldn’t make it big. She used every possible way, every single avenue, but still she couldn’t make it past the bylanes of Hollywood.<br />Enter Toby Temple into Jill Castle’s life. Temptingly, she makes Toby fall for her. Together they begin to rule the roost. Using every single connection that Toby has, Jill virtually reaches the pinnacle of Hollywood.<br />However, her plans are altered when a personal tragedy strikes Toby and he is reduced to a vegetable, good-for-nothing. It is from this moment that Jill shows some semblance of actual care and affection for Toby. While Toby is bed-ridden and has shrunk to a sorry equivalent of an invalid, Jill vows to get him up, bring him back from this sorry excuse of life to his original glory. She does anything and everything to do so when even the doctors had given up and eventually succeeds (to some extent atleast).<br />But there is a catch. By now, she is really fed up of Toby and her sick and disgusting life which she chose for herself. It is at this point of time that Jill’s old flame re-enters into the picture. She deviously plots to kill Toby and murders him. Amidst all this, a secret form Jill’s past comes back to haunt her, a secret which is so explosive that it ends up destroying Jill’s life, completely ruining it leaving it in tatters.<br />Completely devastated by the utter reality of her life’s condition, she runs amok on the deck where she sees Toby’s reflection in the sea. It seemed that Toby was calling him from the other world. Ridden with guilt, she dives into the sea and “joins Toby in the afterlife”?.<br />The novel is explicit in every sense of the word. The steamy scenes, the lustful feelings surrounding the storyline, the darker side of ambition are just not enough to cover for the weak and hackneyed storyline. Although Sidney Sheldon is known for his commercially saleable writing, he always adds tight twists and the plot progresses at a good, if not great, pace. But this time, all there is to the novel is a bleak storyline gift wrapped in lust, desire and ambition.<br /><br />Originally reviewed at <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.vaultofbooks.com" target="_blank">www.vaultofbooks.com</a></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="2299704324132038733">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review" id="review_142728670">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/142728670" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/400931-edy" class="left imgcol" title="Edy"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1297036889p2/400931.jpg" alt="Edy" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/142728670?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jan 22, 2011</a>

      <a href="/user/show/400931-edy" class="user" title="Edy">Edy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it">liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/115130.A_Stranger_In_The_Mirror" title="Paperback 9780006471257" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer142728670">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14235419294484822736">Novel ini memakai setting tahun 1940-1960-an. Novel bercerita tentang Toby Temple, seorang anak laki-laki dari keluarga miskin yang lari ke New York untuk menghindari tanggung jawab karena menghamili teman sekelasnya sewaktu SMA. Toby yang mempunyai bakat menjadi pelawak kemudian berjuang keras untuk masuk ke dunia hiburan. Dengan rasa percaya diri, perjuangan keras, keberuntungan, bakat dan kepandaian berkomunikasi akhirnya dia mulai menapak menjadi artis yang mengorbit di level internasional.</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText14235419294484822736">Novel ini memakai setting tahun 1940-1960-an. Novel bercerita tentang Toby Temple, seorang anak laki-laki dari keluarga miskin yang lari ke New York untuk menghindari tanggung jawab karena menghamili teman sekelasnya sewaktu SMA. Toby yang mempunyai bakat menjadi pelawak kemudian berjuang keras untuk masuk ke dunia hiburan. Dengan rasa percaya diri, perjuangan keras, keberuntungan, bakat dan kepandaian berkomunikasi akhirnya dia mulai menapak menjadi artis yang mengorbit di level internasional. Keberhasilannya itu tidak terlepas dari dukungan manajernya yakni Clifton Lawrence dan tim penulis serta orang2 di belakang layar yang sangat handal. Cuma sayangnya keberhasilan Toby tidak bisa dinikmati oleh ibunya terkasih yang telah meninggal saat Toby masih hidup menggelandang. Sedangkan ayahnya yng hidup di panti jompo dirasakan kurang terlalu dekat baginya. Toby pernah menikah dengan Milli yang seorang wanita simpanan pimpinan mafia, namun pernikahan itu tidak berlangsung indah karena perkawinan itu dilandasi keterpaksaan. Perkawinan itupun terputus karena Millie meninggal ketika melahirkan anak pertamanya yang akhirnya ikut meninggal juga. Dengan bermodal ketenaran dan hartanya, Toby akhirnya lari dari pelukan satu wanita ke wanita lainnya. Toby menjadi terasing dan kesepian di tengah-tengah keberhasilannya.<br /><br />Di sisi lain, novel ini menceritakan nasib Josephine Czinsky seorang gadis cantik keturunan Polandia miskin yang dibesarkan dalam keluarga yang agamis. Josephine remaja mengalami patah hati karena David yang dicintainya menikah dengan orang lain. Josephine kemudian berpetualang ke Hollywood dengan harapan menjadi bintang film. Namun ternyata perjuangannya sangat berat bahkan dia menjadi korban sindikat pembuatan film porno. Josephine yang kemudian berganti nama menjadi Jill kemudian putus asa berusaha menjual diri kepada sutradara atau orang2 film untuk mendapatkan peran di berbagai film.<br /><br />Nasib akhirnya mempertemukan Jill dengan Toby yang saling kesepian. Mereka akhirnya menikah. Namun setelah menikah, Jill memanfaatkan posisinya sebagai istri Toby yang bintang film kelas atas untuk melakukan aksi balas dendam terhadap orang-orang perfilman yang selama ini telah menindasnya. Bahkan dengan semena-mena dia juga memecat Clifton Lawrence yang merupakan manager dan orang yang berperan besar mengatrol karir Toby. Toby yang selalu diforsir kerja keras akhirnya mengalami stroke. Jill dengan rasa cintanya merawat Toby dan timbullah keajaiban dimana Toby bisa sembuh dari stroke. Setelah sembuh dari stroke, Toby melakukan pertunjukan di Eropa termasuk di Moskow. Saat di Moskow, Toby kembali mengalami stroke yang lebih parah. Di Moskow ini Jill sebelum pulang ke Hollywood, sempat bertemu David yang sudah menjadi milyarder muda. <br /><br />Toby semakin hari semakin parah sakitnya. Di sisi lain Jill, mulai terpikat kembali dengan David. Jill kemudian melakukan pembunuhan berencana terhadap Toby yang tidak berdaya dengan mendorong Toby dan kursi roda masuk ke kolam renang. Setelah Toby meninggal, Jill akan menikah dengan David. Namun rencana pernikahan yang sudah direncanakan menjadi batal karena David shock mengetahui bahwa Jill pernah main di film porno. Jillpun akhirnya bunuh diri dengan kegagalan cintanya ini....<br /><br />Menurut saya, novel ini tidak terlalu istimewa dengan alur yang mudah ditebak dan datar. Jadi jangan berharap memperoleh hikmah pembelajaran atau inspirasi yang dalam dari novel ini..... <br /></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="14235419294484822736">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span style="display:none" id="freeText5891518779410710111">This being my first Sheldon read, has proven to be a disappointment and I have decided to never include his works in my future reads. This novel juggles with a handful of words through out the novel and this repetitiveness, becomes unbearable after a point. This novel is just like those sleazy movies with nothing to offer but sex. The theme of this novel is a mystery to me because of the fact that an industrious, painstaking artist who worked his ass of through out his prime age, with a meagre earning and distress being his constant acquaintance, emerged to be the most successful star in the unruly universe of Hollywood and survived, but amidst a healthy, buoyant life, a beautiful and loving wife to accompany him is with, is gravely affected by series of strokes that paralyses him and takes from him his most precious gift, his voice. And this happens as the book suggests because of his back- breaking work schedule. Bull shit. An once this devoted wife, cheats of her husband with her high school lover and blah blah blah. This novel should not be called a novel because it has nothing novel to offer. It sucks. Do not read it, i repeat do not read it... </span>

              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1245377962">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12916160797081950042">Sidney sheldon ini seperti tuhan dia menentukan nasib manusia. Mulai dari lahirnya, matinya, keterpurukannya, kesuksesannya, perjumpaannya dan perpisahannya. Nasib manusia ditampilkan seperti roller coster naik, turun, menikung, serta jungkir balik. Yang menarik adalah perubahan nasib tokoh-tokoh di novel ini mulai dari latar belakang masa kecilnya yang sederhana dan miskin kemudian perjuangan untuk menjadi bintang besar yang melalui berbagai rintangan sampai ke kondisi yang amat tragis. <br /><br />Latar w</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText12916160797081950042">Sidney sheldon ini seperti tuhan dia menentukan nasib manusia. Mulai dari lahirnya, matinya, keterpurukannya, kesuksesannya, perjumpaannya dan perpisahannya. Nasib manusia ditampilkan seperti roller coster naik, turun, menikung, serta jungkir balik. Yang menarik adalah perubahan nasib tokoh-tokoh di novel ini mulai dari latar belakang masa kecilnya yang sederhana dan miskin kemudian perjuangan untuk menjadi bintang besar yang melalui berbagai rintangan sampai ke kondisi yang amat tragis. <br /><br />Latar waktunya terjadi selama 50 tahun mulai thn 1919 sampai 1969 namun hanya ditampilkan dalam 444 halaman. Kejadian-kejadiannya banyak yang dipaparkan sebagai rangkaian, beberapa adegan terasa terlalu cepat seperti ada proses yang hilang contohnya adegan Cisy yang mengendarai mobil dalam kecepatan tinggi sehingga masuk jurang dan David yang mengejarnya kemudian menolongnya tiba2 sudah ada dipintu mobil. Harusnya bisa ditampilkan proses perjalanan David menuju jurang agar tidak terasa adanya lompatan adegan.<br /><br />Yang menarik dalam mengkikuti perjalanan hidup dua karakter utamanya yaitu Tobi Temple dan Jill Castle adalah kita diajak memasuki dunia bisnis pertunjukan di Hollywood. Ternyata dunia tersebut begitu kejam alias tidak seindah yang dibayangkan oleh manusia2 yang bercita-cita menjadi bintang tenar. Sisi gelap Hollywood menjadi kenyataan yang harus dijalani oleh orang-orang yang tidak beruntung. Persaingan menjadi bintang sangat berat, begitu banyak perempuan cantik bertubuh molek berkumpul di tempat ini namun tetap saja banyak yang tidak mendapatkan peran alias menganggur sehingga diantara mereka harus bekerja serabutan sekedar buat menyambung hidup. Demi mendapatkan peran lewat jalan pintas beberapa aktris terpaksa menjual tubuhnya kepada casting director, karena casting director lah yang menentukan seorang aktor atau aktris bisa bermain dalam sebuah film.<br /><br />Secara keseluruhan saya menyukai buku ini. Sidney Sheldon memang terampil memainkan emosi pembacanya, beberapa kali saya merasakan juga apa yang dirasakan oleh karakter-karakter yang ada di novel ini.</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="12916160797081950042">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer8695904088945648810">The big bad story of Hollywood land, the reality, the struggle,rise to power and the great fall together create this book.<br /><br />A not so typical crime thriller it's a commercialized story with past, present and future working together for two people. The story is fast,witty,glamorous and the reality binds well with fiction. The build up to the main content is catchy. The character sketch done well and gelled perfectly.<br /><br />The predictability very high and the end failed to live up to the expectations. The</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8695904088945648810">The big bad story of Hollywood land, the reality, the struggle,rise to power and the great fall together create this book.<br /><br />A not so typical crime thriller it's a commercialized story with past, present and future working together for two people. The story is fast,witty,glamorous and the reality binds well with fiction. The build up to the main content is catchy. The character sketch done well and gelled perfectly.<br /><br />The predictability very high and the end failed to live up to the expectations. The hidden motive factor found missing and story becoming flat.<br /><br />The story can be liked for the characters but not the story line. The glitz and glamour weave the magic but it wanes off too soon.<br /><br />A good book but not so like the author's other works.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11704698137359320533">I was really debating with myself if I should give this book a 3 or 4 star. I really love some parts of this book, esp. Toby and Jill's love story.   <span style="display:none" id="freeText11704698137359320533">I was really debating with myself if I should give this book a 3 or 4 star. I really love some parts of this book, esp. Toby and Jill's love story. I thought it was a hair-raising kind. Just thinking of love that made one come back from the dead. I cried when Toby got up from his vegetable state, walked on his own and cried "Jillll...." when he didn't see Jill as she was so bone-deep exhausted and sick. He must have thought something bad happened to her and his deep love for her made him get up and look for her. That was really incredible, a test that showed what true love could do.<br /><br />The only thing that I didn't like so much is the amorality of the main characters. They were vengeful, wicked, ungrateful.<br /><br />Sheldon's portrayal of the showbiz world was simply staggering and informative. Well, he was in that business for decades, so he knew what he was talking about.<br /><br />Nonetheless, Sheldon has done it again! The twists were so unexpected, I didn't see Jill's last cruel action and David's secret coming.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/10372022-andrea-ika?shelf=wishlist" class="actionLinkLite">wishlist</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer772318495">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18203624024067517212">A Stranger in the Mirror (1976)<br />by Sidney Sheldon (Author)<br /><br />Blurb<br />Toby Temple is a super star and a super bastard, a man adored by his fans and plagued by suspicion and distrust.<br />Jil lClastle came to Hollywood to be a star--- and discovered that she had to but her way with her body.<br />Now this lonely man and this disillusioned woman find themselves bound to each other by a love so ruthless, so strong, it will destroy everyone who gets in its way.<br /><br />Review<br />This book really takes you into the personal lives o</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText18203624024067517212">A Stranger in the Mirror (1976)<br />by Sidney Sheldon (Author)<br /><br />Blurb<br />Toby Temple is a super star and a super bastard, a man adored by his fans and plagued by suspicion and distrust.<br />Jil lClastle came to Hollywood to be a star--- and discovered that she had to but her way with her body.<br />Now this lonely man and this disillusioned woman find themselves bound to each other by a love so ruthless, so strong, it will destroy everyone who gets in its way.<br /><br />Review<br />This book really takes you into the personal lives of the most Hollywood actors and actress ...how they coped up with the ups and highs...how they proved their talents and how they cracked the nutshell in impressing the directors... and out of this... we feel like watching a Typical Hollywood Movie about cine stars.. Toby Temple, a stand-up comedian who was unlucky enough to get his mother all through his life.. held his urge to not to go to his place from the Hollywood because of his past sexual acts.. After his endless efforts to possess the status he wanted ... he became a star to superstar...and Josephine... who change her name as Jill Castle... marry's him after Toby's excessive seduction towards to her... Ofcourse Jill plan was not loving him actually but to take the revenge which produced from the vengeance towards to the cine industry people who took a chance to play brutal games on her.. In simple words, Toby was just a pawn to make her plans get succeed...<br /><br />This novel is a departure for Sidney Sheldon, who usually writes thrillers with beautiful, young heroines facing disaster every few pages<br /> It has a very fast-pace and yet the ending was not what I have expected--it is unpredictable to me at least.<br />This is a well-written, exciting story about the world of actors, agents, and directors. Its shows the dark side of Hollywood.<br />This book was written in 1976, but it could still be true about Hollywood now, or in another 50 years. I learned that one that has fame and wealth is infinitely poorer then one who has friends and honesty. This book does have some inappropriate parts so I wouldn’t recommend it as a school read, but if anyone enjoys a good life story novel or an out of the box read, this book is certainly worth the time. <br />Final rating : 3,5/5 stars<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="18203624024067517212">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing">it was amazing</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was amazing"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer760639301">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1008241133467840095">Every coin has two sides. If you think Toby Temple is just a plain jerk when you start reading the book,you might be wrong because he's the kind of person who's willing to waive medical bills of a dying person.But he's still a jerk,who manipulate others to feed his own insecurities. After making a teen pregnant during high school,Toby fled away from his hometown and his sin to pursue his mother's dream to see him successful someday. Meanwhile on the other end, Josephine Czinski changed her name</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText1008241133467840095">Every coin has two sides. If you think Toby Temple is just a plain jerk when you start reading the book,you might be wrong because he's the kind of person who's willing to waive medical bills of a dying person.But he's still a jerk,who manipulate others to feed his own insecurities. After making a teen pregnant during high school,Toby fled away from his hometown and his sin to pursue his mother's dream to see him successful someday. Meanwhile on the other end, Josephine Czinski changed her name to Jill Castle and fled away from her hometown to mend her broken heart after she saw her mother bringing the old wedding dress for the wedding of David Kenyon and Cissy Topping. <br /><br />There's not much difference between Jill and Toby. Both of them are very much the same,full of vengeance and ill feelings towards the world. <br /><br />The story took a twist when Toby met Jill,together they rule Hollywood and show the world the dark side of the show business.At the end of the story,revenge outruled peace and happiness. Sad to see Toby and Jill's life ended in a very sad way.Both of them were eaten by their own creed and vengeance.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9950042601054691670">A<a rel="nofollow" href="http://www" target="_blank">www</a>... buku ini bahkan pertama kali terbit jauuuh lebih tua dari aku :))<br />tahun 1976!! Buku ini luar biasa bagus, asal tahu saja ya, aku menemukan buku ini di sebuah pasar loak yang penjualnya memperlakukan buku2 dagangannya seperti setumpukan koran bekas :( warnanya telah menguning dimakan usia, bahkan bentuk bukunya sudah melengkung dan tidak simetris lagi.   <span style="display:none" id="freeText9950042601054691670">A<a rel="nofollow" href="http://www" target="_blank">www</a>... buku ini bahkan pertama kali terbit jauuuh lebih tua dari aku :))<br />tahun 1976!! Buku ini luar biasa bagus, asal tahu saja ya, aku menemukan buku ini di sebuah pasar loak yang penjualnya memperlakukan buku2 dagangannya seperti setumpukan koran bekas :( warnanya telah menguning dimakan usia, bahkan bentuk bukunya sudah melengkung dan tidak simetris lagi. Sayang sekaliii :(<br /><br />Ini kisah hidup sepasang manusia yang merangkak dari bawah demi mencapai impiannya masuk ke dalam ranah perfilman Hollywood yang kejam, penuh intrik, kepalsuan dan menuntut pengorbanan harga diri yang mungkin tak lagi mampu terbeli walaupun uang telah ditaklukkan oleh keduanya.<br /><br />Dua orang dengan jenis kelamin dan latar belakang yang berbeda, sedikit demi sedikit merangkak keluar dari dunia nyata menuju dream land mereka. Sang lelaki berusaha merintis kariernya di dunia stand up commedy, dan si perempuan berjuang menjadi artis nomor 1 Hollywood. Terpaut usia yang jauh tidak membuat mereka mundur, dan ketika mereka bersatu, berdua mereka menundukkan Hollywood dan membalas kekejaman yang pernah mereka terima ketika mereka masih berada di bawah dan menjadi alas kaki orang-orang yang sekarang berada di bawah kaki mereka. <br /><br />Namun mungkin karena mereka terlalu larut dalam dendam, kehampaandan kekerdilan jiwa, dan terlena dalam gemerlap, pujian dan harta serta tahta, karma membuat mereka hancur, saling menyakiti dan akhirnya binasa... Kita tidak tahu apa yang akan menimpa kita nanti....</span>

<div itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope="" itemprop="reviews" class="review nosyndicate" id="review_163166303">
  <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/163166303" itemprop="url" />
  <a href="/user/show/5273390-laini" class="left imgcol" title="Laini"><img src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1303486205p2/5273390.jpg" alt="Laini" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a href="/review/show/163166303?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Oct 15, 2011</a>

      <a href="/user/show/5273390-laini" class="user" title="Laini">Laini</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok">it was ok</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="it was ok"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/115130.A_Stranger_In_The_Mirror" title="Paperback 9780006471257" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/5273390-laini?shelf=fiction" class="actionLinkLite">fiction</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/5273390-laini?shelf=mystery" class="actionLinkLite">mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer163166303">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13279954320895203269">A Stranger in the Mirror is a hard book to describe. The basic story is split in 2 for most of the book. Toby Temple begins the tale, he is a very famous and very successful actor/comedian in Hollywood. However the story starts with his early life. He left home very young as he had impregnated a girl at his school whose parents were looking for a shotgun wedding, so with his own mother's blessing he fled. He worked for many years trying to make it big and finally did. <br /><br />Meanwhile, we have Jill Cas</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText13279954320895203269">A Stranger in the Mirror is a hard book to describe. The basic story is split in 2 for most of the book. Toby Temple begins the tale, he is a very famous and very successful actor/comedian in Hollywood. However the story starts with his early life. He left home very young as he had impregnated a girl at his school whose parents were looking for a shotgun wedding, so with his own mother's blessing he fled. He worked for many years trying to make it big and finally did. <br /><br />Meanwhile, we have Jill Castle, her upbringing was very tough, with a fiercely religious mother, she struggled with blinding headaches all her life. <br /><br />The majority of the story is about the early lives of these 2 main characters. I don't think they actually meet until after two thirds of the book is over. But despite the fact that we have spent so much time reading about them, I still didn't feel as strongly for them as I should have done. Maybe it was supposed to be like that. Maybe we aren't really supposed to like these people.<br /><br />Toby becomes an arrogant, rude man who uses people to get where he wants, and at the same time is incredibly lonely. Jill, even though she has struggled and been used and abused horrifically herself in her search for stardom, isn't likeable either. Instead of her experiences making her a sympathetic character, she becomes vengeful, and hateful. She also uses people to get what she wants and in that way, the 2 characters are made for each other, however can a relationship like that survive? Well to find out you'll just have to read it yourself!</span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="13279954320895203269">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a href="/review/show/1350352413?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate" class="reviewDate createdAt right">Jul 31, 2015</a>

      <a href="/user/show/13334999-frances-rivers" class="user" title="Frances Rivers">Frances Rivers</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars"><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it">really liked it</span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p10" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span><span class="staticStar p0" size="15x15" title="really liked it"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText"> · </span>
          <a href="/book/show/115130.A_Stranger_In_The_Mirror" title="Paperback 9780006471257" class="lightGreyText">review of another edition</a>


        


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a href="/review/list/13334999-frances-rivers?shelf=classics" class="actionLinkLite">classics</a>, 
              <a href="/review/list/13334999-frances-rivers?shelf=heart-wrenching" class="actionLinkLite">heart-wrenching</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span style="" class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer1350352413">
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8282845992947345118">Riveting plot twists as always, superb story writing. Most graphic Sheldon novel I've read so far but it speaks a lot of truth on the trashiness of Hollywood industries. The loneliness of Toby &amp; Josephine tripled the pace for climaxes and conflicts and its just really..lugubrious. As much of the just ending did not leave me completely depressed Sheldon will always be that stupendous and brilliant writer ever since I read "Tomorrow Never Comes". </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zuNI+3tKF7XxEBxKc/6gu+BBVZk1TDp/ouRQIavjp3KrN3coiZgDT33IaPENn0YJqbaWgHyRfdXI7VWzZ3ZRNw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('t2ZRbxe78V3BM21FBL4mE4dps1Udd7o57RDMb78EVCXSsm685Wnlp03rGf5638Chzp5wTFSq/ZOHGcn9c5GiYA==')})
  }

    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/9068.Sidney_Sheldon">About Sidney Sheldon</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/9068.Sidney_Sheldon"><img alt="9068" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1209169297p2/9068.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer8073063722487354305">Was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist. His TV works spanned a 20-year period during which he created I Dream of Jeannie (1965-70), Hart to Hart (1979-84), and The Patty Duke Show (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as Master of the Gam</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText8073063722487354305">Was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist. His TV works spanned a 20-year period during which he created I Dream of Jeannie (1965-70), Hart to Hart (1979-84), and The Patty Duke Show (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as Master of the Game (1982), The Other Side of Midnight (1973) and Rage of Angels (1980) that he became most famous.</span>
